Sojitz Corporation Integrated Report 2019 1 INTRODUCTION Corporate Statement/To Our Stakeholders Utilizing innovative ideas, Sojitz will continue to take on new challenges, connecting steady growth to the next leap forward. Sojitz Group Statement Since its founding, Sojitz has continued to learn from the past, take on new challenges, and achieve one goal after The Sojitz Group creates value and prosperity by another. This has forged a “Sojitz Identity” defined by genba-ryoku*—that is, the abilities exhibited by our people connecting the world with a spirit of integrity. on the business frontlines. It is the very culmination of the business ingenuity honed by our predecessors, the capacity for disciplined growth developed from the lessons learned during our hardest times, and the creativity which will lead the way to the future. Sojitz Group Slogan Medium-term Management Plan 2020 – Commitment to Growth – began in April 2018, and during our first year of the plan, we successfully linked our past efforts to new profit and maintained fiscal discipline in continuing to replace assets and conduct new investments and loans. We made full use of our greatest advantages and abilities to actively challenge new business areas, hand-in-hand with our Sojitz Guiding Principles trusted partners, while responding to the dizzying changes of the business environment. The Sojitz Group aims to create value for our stakeholders by This year as well, we will continue to refine our aligning our strong, capable individuals under the following 5 principles: strengths to build new “clusters of revenue-generating business,” reaffirm our “Commitment to Growth,” and realize steady 1. Trust: Build enduring trust. profit growth of around 10% per year. Sojitz is now in a stage of growth. Seeking 2. Innovation: Innovate with foresight. to maximize the “two types of value”— value for 3. Speed: Strive for speed. Sojitz” and “value for society”—all of us at Sojitz will unite to achieve sustainable growth for our 4. Challenge: Take calculated risks. company and create a more prosperous society. 5. Perseverance: Persevere until successful. The Group mitigates such credit risk by objectively assigning credit ratings to the customers to which it extends credit based on the Adjustment made at the start of IFRS 9 ....................................................................... 121 — 121 Company's credit rating system. The Group also controls credit risk by setting rating-based credit limits on a customer-by-customer basis Balance as of April 1, 2018 based on IFRS 9 .............................................................. 647 37,695 38,342 and enforcing the credit limits thus set. The Group employs other safeguards (e.g., collaterals and guarantees) as warranted by the customer's creditworthiness. Additionally, the Group has a system for assessing receivables, in which customers are extracted based on a Reclassified as allowance for doubtful accounts against credit impaired financial assets .............................................................................................................
